# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="bc90f-102">Membres obsolètes dans le cadre .NET</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bc90f-102">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bc90f-103">Cet article répertorie les membres de type qui sont obsolètes dans .NET Framework 4.5 et les versions ultérieures.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bc90f-103">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bc90f-104">Les membres de type sont regroupés par assemblée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bc90f-104">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bc90f-105">Cet article ne liste pas les membres des types obsolètes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bc90f-105">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bc90f-106">Pour une liste de types obsolètes, voir [les types obsolètes](obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bc90f-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>
